🟪 French toast Dream insight (L) 💭🍞 |In| :: Had a dream that I was in an exam/presentation type situation and was told to write my 'essay' on 3 pieces of French toast.. I tried to carefully make out letters with a ball point pen, but quickly realized that was futile. Lesson= eat the french toast, and then use the calories to go find a better solution! It's a perfect analogy to the old game - we're often told to do something that doesn't really work and if we have the courage to say "no, there's a better way" we'll find it.

🟧🟧 Stories people are ready for now 💡🤯 |+E|{EP}:: Insights on how the biggest vision stories we want to tell are often not 'believable' by most people because they can't touch the higher consciousness views. Instead the  incremental, 10% better stories are relatable now. But we can't get stuck there - of course we need people who are seeing and working on the biggest visions. Making smaller steps that are accessible to people's limiting beliefs now helps get traction. Underpromise, Overdeliver.

Changing designs without changing the game won't deliver solutions people are after.

🟧🟧 Talk about New Game flow 🗣🔄 |+E|{EP}:: Talked about true P2P design and how that affects the flow of value/ money. Walked through examples of giving to frames with intention of rewarding past value blocks (which is an uncommon notion) and also how choosing to give a large amount for the future is different when there's no central authority holding it. It's given, but in a way that the person giving can decide their openess to give backs and conditions of blocks to reward.

🟧🟧 The Why vs. What order insight 💡|+E|{EP}:: We live in a world that has been trained to focus on the 'what' so much that everything is designed with that priority, and the 'why' or depth and meaning is an afterthought... which is backwards and never really possible. You can't build something and then try to add the 'magic' later. It's what was always challenging and frustrating about marketing- being asked to add the magic to something that was lacking it.

🟧 Secure "portal.gift" domain (B) 🕳️🎁 |+E|{EP1} :: One of the powerful components in the giving economy is the super easy ability to "give liquid stored value" at any level.  At the level of a "value block", "group", "cooperative frame", or "person frame" level.  The most basic element here is a super easy "portal", typically a QR code address to give to.  This basic component can exist anywhere on the web, embedded in media, or even in physical form in the world.  We're build the open source backend and front end to support all this.  Initially bitcoin can be given, and as soon as it is live, we'll enable giving of "Gratitude" digital assets.

🟧 Magic of Money with No "Payments" (B) 💸 |Giv| :: Reflected on why using "money" to buy other people's time & resources is not the same as "unilateral giving", where we give freely.  The polluted feeling many people have around money is partly because it has usually been possible to make people do things that are against their personal well being when it is used incorrectly.  For happiness to be associated with the concept of money, a circular system of unilateral giving is optimal. This is the "new economy" we refer to often, it could also be seen as only a "forward flow" of financial resources that flow to those in need or to the projects that benefit the world the most.  There are no "payments" in this system, and  "profit" is not the goal, giving is the goal.
